# Decision Log â€” Mission Control

Product, design and technical decisions for Mission Control (the Next.js app). Most recent on top. See the index and format in [DECISION-LOG.md](../../DECISION-LOG.md).

> The live project state is in [.pandacorp/status.yaml](../.pandacorp/status.yaml); the PRD in [docs/product/prd.md](product/prd.md) and the FRDs in [docs/frds/](frds/). This is where the **why** of the decisions goes, not the state.

## 2026-06-30 â€” Party factory-off survives the SSE replay (PartyLiveShell, AC-06-013.4 follow-up)
**What:** Follow-up to the same-day factory-off fix. The server (`PartyTab`) correctly rendered the powered-off scene from `status.yaml running:false`, but AFTER hydration the scene re-activated: `PartyLiveShell` re-derives the snapshot from each SSE frame via `toFraguaSnapshot`, and `/api/live` emits the current event tail on connect even when the build is OFF â†’ `liveFrame` becomes non-null with the STALE tail â†’ the re-derive ran WITHOUT `running` â†’ `active:true` again (phantom WO + lit beat returned). Fix: thread `running` into `PartyLiveShell`; in the re-derive, a frame whose `lastEventAt` is NOT newer than the page-load snapshot is treated as a mere replay and keeps `running:false` (powered-off); a genuinely newer event (ISO-8601 `>`) reactivates (the build resumed, AC-06-013.3). `PartyTab` passes `running` to `PartyLiveShell`.
**Why:** Verified on `:1987` after the first fix: SSR HTML showed 0 running sprites (off, correct) but the hydrated client showed `runningSprites:1` + `litBeats:2` â€” the SSE replay undid the server's factory-off. The initial fix only covered the RSC snapshot, not the live re-derive. Caught by a browser check, not the unit gate (the unit test exercised the pure snapshot, not the SSE path). Added a `PartyLiveShell` test that mocks `useLiveSnapshot` with a stale replay vs a fresher event.
**Impact:** Code: `â€¦/_party/PartyTab/PartyLiveShell.tsx` (+`running` prop, replay-vs-fresher logic), `â€¦/_party/PartyTab/PartyTab.tsx` (pass `running`). Tests: `PartyLiveShell.factoryoff.test.tsx` (NEW). Same AC-06-013.4 contract; no new doc surface.

## 2026-06-30 â€” Manual (Cأ³dice del gremio) actualizado: rename architecture + digest + pestaأ±a Arquitectura (DR-046)
**What:** Sincronizado el Manual con los cambios de esta tanda (DR-046: el Manual refleja la superficie operable). (1) `concepts/el-pipeline.md` آ§3: el encabezado "Architecture (Blueprint)" â†’ "Architecture"; se documenta que la fase emite `.pandacorp/comms/arquitectura-resumen.md` y que MC lo renderiza en la pestaأ±a **Arquitectura** (stack, modelo de datos con rama "Sin BD", servicios, ADRs/env en vivo, plan de implementaciأ³n como DAG, ficha por-FRD con sub-DAG); nota explأ­cita del rename `/blueprint`â†’`/architecture` y de que el artefacto `blueprint.md` por-FRD conserva su nombre. (2) `concepts/mission-control-por-dentro.md`: nueva secciأ³n "La card de una idea" con las pestaأ±as del detalle del tablero (Propuesta آ· Spec آ· Arquitectura آ· Documentos آ· Campaأ±a) y su condiciأ³n de apariciأ³n por fase; + fila `lib/architecture/*` en la tabla de lectores (`arquitectura-resumen.md` + `docs/adr/*` + `.env.example`).
**Why:** El owner pidiأ³ actualizar la documentaciأ³n de Mission Control tras el rename del skill, el digest de arquitectura y el tab. El catأ،logo de skills del Manual auto-deriva (el comando renombrado ya aparece solo); estas son las pأ،ginas narrativas hand-authored que no auto-derivan.
**Context:** Sin cambio de cأ³digo; markdown del Manual (`content/manual/`). El test de contenido (`wo-08-005.content.test.ts`) sigue verde (asserts laxos: fases + `blueprint.md`). No toquأ© la fase "operation" del diagrama (drift de DR-085, ajeno a esta tanda).
**Impact:** `content/manual/concepts/el-pipeline.md`, `content/manual/concepts/mission-control-por-dentro.md`. Fأ،brica: أ­ndice de templates `plugin/templates/docs/README.md` (digests + "Generated by", v9.33.2 â€” ver `plugin/docs/decision-log.md`).

## 2026-06-30 â€” DAG de dependencias por-FRD dentro del modal de cada FRD (Arquitectura tab, AC-02-013.6)
**What:** En el tab Arquitectura, al abrir el modal de un FRD, ahora se muestra al final un **DAG acotado a
ese FRD** â€”reutilizando el mismo `WoDag` del Plan de implementaciأ³nâ€” con solo las work orders de ese FRD y
sus dependencias/paralelismo intra-FRD. Solo aparece cuando el FRD tiene **mأ،s de una** work order (con una
sola no hay nada que graficar, asأ­ que se omite). Las WOs por FRD se cruzan con las live `workOrders`
(`listWorkOrders`) por nأ؛mero de FRD (`workOrdersForFrd` + `frdKey`: "FRD-01" â†” "frd-01-â€¦"); el DAG dropea
las deps cross-FRD (esos nodos no estأ،n en el subconjunto), mostrando la cadena interna del FRD.
**Why:** Pedido del dueأ±o: ver dependencias y paralelismo de cada FRD sin tener que escanear el DAG global;
y que no aparezca para FRDs de una sola WO. Reutiliza el componente existente (cero librerأ­a nueva, DR-062).
**Context:** Verificado contra `personal-page-v2`: FRD-01 (4 WOs) muestra el DAG con su cadena
WO-01-001â†’â€¦; los FRDs de 1 WO (Home, Contact, â€¦) no lo muestran. Tests: `ArchitectureDigest.test.tsx`
(gating >1 vs 1 WO, DAG acotado a las WOs del FRD).
**Impact:** Cأ³digo: `src/app/board/_components/CardDetail/ArchitectureDigest/ArchitectureDigest.tsx`
(`workOrdersForFrd`/`frdKey` + `FrdModal` con DAG condicional). Doc canأ³nico: `frd-02-ideas-board/frd.md`
(AC-02-013.6). Extiende REQ-02-013. Sin cambio de plugin (solo MC).

## 2026-06-30 â€” Party: factory-off from `status.yaml running` (AC-06-013.4) + bridges below the rooms
**What:** Two Party (La Fragua) bug fixes. **(1) Factory-off detection.** `toFraguaSnapshot` set `active: true` whenever the event tail had a FRD â€” with NO freshness/running check. The `~/.claude/dashboard-events.ndjson` keeps the LAST build's events forever, so after a build finished the scene stayed "active": a frozen lit "Oleada" beat + a phantom running WO (the final Visual-QA pass). Fix: thread the project's authoritative `running` flag (already read in `ProjectWorkspace` from `status.yaml`) â†’ `PartyTab` â†’ `toFraguaSnapshot`; when `running === false` the snapshot is forced to the powered-off state (`active:false`, `running:[]`, gate closed). `PartyTab` now gates scene-vs-empty on **`frd !== null`** (a build EXISTS) instead of `active`, so an OFF build still renders the scene's grey powered-off design (the `PowerOffOverlay`, AC-06-013) rather than the never-built empty state; and `PartyScene` lights NO flow-strip beat when off (`activeKeys = active ? â€¦ : []`). The SSE re-derive (`PartyLiveShell`) deliberately does NOT receive `running` â€” a live event frame means the build IS active, so a stale page-load `running` must not suppress a build that just started. Known nuance: a build that stops WHILE the tab is open updates on the next RSC render (reload/nav), not instantly â€” acceptable per AC-06-013.3 (events resume â†’ active). **(2) Stone bridges z-order.** The bridges' endpoints overlap the room rectangles (coords 415â€“505 over forge 16â€“448 + tribunal 472+), and at the prototype's `z-index:2` they sat visibly ON TOP of the room art. Owner-requested: bridges BELOW the rooms. Lowered `StoneBridge` root `z-index` 2â†’0 (above only the stage grid; rooms are z-index 1, sprites z-index 5) and updated the prototype `la-fragua.html .bridge` to match.
**Why:** Owner testing on `:3000`/main with the factory OFF: "se quedأ³ congeladoâ€¦ aparece un work order Visual QA que no deberأ­aâ€¦ si la fأ،brica estأ، apagada deberأ­amos mostrar el diseأ±o de fأ،brica apagada"; and "los puentes deberأ­an aparecer abajo de las imأ،genes de las salas, ahorita aparecen encima". Root cause of (1): event-presence â‰  build-running; only `status.yaml running` distinguishes them. Found while testing (bugs), fixed directly in an isolated worktree (DR-096) with TDD.
**Impact:** Code: `â€¦/_party/fragua-snapshot/fragua-snapshot.ts` (`running` opt â†’ factory-off), `â€¦/_party/PartyTab/PartyTab.tsx` (`running` prop + `frd`-gated body), `â€¦/projects/[slug]/ProjectWorkspace.tsx` (pass `running`), `â€¦/_party/PartyScene/PartyScene.tsx` (no lit beats when off), `components/modules/party/StoneBridge/StoneBridge.tsx` (z-index 0). Docs: `frd-06-party/frd.md` (AC-06-013.4), `frd-06-party/mocks/la-fragua.html` (`.bridge` z-index). Tests: `fragua-snapshot.factoryoff.test.ts` (NEW), `StoneBridge.test.tsx` (+z-index). No Party visual baseline exists, so the z-order change trips no visual gate.

Bumped `overlay_version` to 8.49.0. `e2e/_target.ts` (per-project, not byte-synced) was unchanged and already exports the symbols the new spec needs.

## 2026-06-30 â€” Eliminado `docs/proposals/` en MC; regla reforzada en fأ،brica y proyecto
**What:** Deleted `mission-control/docs/proposals/architecture-tab-and-skill-rename.md` (stale context doc â€” the work was already shipped in commit `56e31f7`). Removed the empty `docs/proposals/` folder. Added an explicit "Forbidden pattern" prohibition to `factory/standards/documentation.md` and to `docs/rules/documentation-and-decisions.md`: a project **never** has `docs/proposals/`; pending changes always go to `.pandacorp/inbox/changes/` via `/pandacorp:change`.
**Why:** An agent created the folder as a "context doc for an implementation session" instead of using the change inbox. The file was invisible to the build engine and Mission Control's queue, so it would never have been automatically picked up. The rule needed to be written explicitly because the documentation standard listed what *was* allowed but never said what was forbidden.
**Impact:** `factory/standards/documentation.md` (new "Forbidden pattern" section); `docs/rules/documentation-and-decisions.md` (same); deleted `docs/proposals/` folder.

## 2026-06-30 â€” Factory-flow audit: overlay upgrade + doc-drift reconciliation (operationâ†’release, FRD-15 semver, Playwright)
**What:** Applied the Mission-Control findings of the factory-flow audit (`docs/proposals/19-factory-flow-audit-2026-06-30.md`):
- **Overlay upgraded 8.44.0 â†’ 8.48.0 + DR-100 gate installed (P0-1/P0-2).** `.pandacorp/verify.sh` was behind the canonical Next.js template and **missed the DR-100 residual-ambiguity gate** (a `[NEEDS CLARIFICATION]` marker in an `status: ACTIVE` doc must RED). Synced `verify.sh` verbatim to the template (adds the DR-100 block) and re-synced the other managed overlay scripts (`pending-work.sh`, `merge-queue.sh` â€” now carrying the audit's JSON-escaping + busy-main preflight hardening). Verified MC carries no `[NEEDS CLARIFICATION]` in an ACTIVE doc, so the new gate doesn't red-lock the build. Bumped `overlay_version` to 8.48.0 and the `guide.md` pipeline line off the obsolete `operation` phase.
- **`operation` phase swept from FRD docs + prototype (P0-3).** DR-085 had folded `operation` into `release` in the code (the `Phase` type is `product|design|architecture|implementation|release`; active set `architecture|implementation|release`; `release`â†’shipped column), but FRD-01/02/03/04/09 docs and `docs/design/prototype/index.html` still listed `operation` as a live phase/Phase-union value/active-set member/command key. Corrected all current-state assertions to match the code; preserved the "DR-085: operation folded into release" history. (Files: frd-01 blueprint + wo-01-005; frd-02 frd/fdd/blueprint + wo-02-001/003/011; frd-03 blueprint + wo-03-001; frd-04 blueprint + wo-04-003; frd-09 wo-09-001; prototype index.html.)
- **FRD-15 reconciled to the semver model (P0-4).** `frd.md` was already amended (2026-06-22) to compare installed vs source plugin **semver `version`** (the signal `claude plugin update` uses), but the `blueprint.md` and `work-orders/` still described the abandoned git-commit-SHA + dirty-state model (frozen installed SHA â†’ permanent false "behind" alarm). Rewrote them to the semver contract (`readInstalledVersion`/`readPluginSourceVersion`/`getPluginSyncState`, reasons behind/in-sync/unknown, banner only on "behind", null-on-unreadable); retired REQ-15-001/REQ-15-003; SHA model kept only as labelled history.
- **Architecture + PRD reconciled (P1-1/P1-12).** `docs/product/architecture.md` now reflects the real fail-closed gate chain and the four Playwright browser gates (smoke DR-055, visual DR-056, responsive DR-074, shell DR-075) instead of "no Playwright/e2e in v1"; the phase enum dropped `operation`; plugin-sync described as semver, not SHA. The bounded-write set (discard/restore `status` ADR-0002, visual `favorite` ADR-0003) is now stated consistently in architecture and PRD (the PRD no longer frames discard as the only write).
- **`docs/api.md` reconciled (P2).** Hand-maintained (no generator found). Removed `operation` as a live phase everywhere (Phase union, `workspaceCommands`, `activeProjects`, `deriveColumn`, `nextStep`, FRD-12 KPI) and replaced the plugin-sync SHA description with the semver contract; fixed two latent current-state errors surfaced during the sweep (`deriveColumn` `release`â†’shipped, `nextStep` `release`â†’`/pandacorp:iterate`), verified against the live `lib/` modules.
- **Pending-queue items classified (P1-10).** `phase: release` with `pending_decisions: 1` + `pending_changes: 8` is **not** unfinished work hiding behind green: `pending_changes` = 5 `ready` + 3 `draft` post-release backlog (already classified in the gitignored `.pandacorp/inbox/changes/README.md`); `pending_decisions: 1` is WO-03-002 (owner resolved it Option A; the action is in-flight). Surfacing these in the MC UI is already captured as the backlog item `mc-pending-items-view.md`. No counters were touched (an active parallel session owns the WO-03-002 work â€” DR-099).
**Why:** P0â€“P2 documentation-drift findings â€” canonical docs that name a phase the code no longer has, or a plugin-sync model the code abandoned, mislead any agent/skill reading them and break the FRDâ†”code traceability spine; the overlay was behind the current gate standard.
**Impact:** `.pandacorp/{verify.sh,pending-work.sh,merge-queue.sh,status.yaml,guide.md}`; `docs/product/{architecture.md,prd.md}`; `docs/api.md`; FRD-01/02/03/04/09 docs + work-orders; FRD-15 blueprint + work-orders; `docs/design/prototype/index.html`. ## 2026-06-29 â€” Fix: el deep-link `/projects/[slug]` daba 404 para TODOS los proyectos
**What:** La pأ،gina de workspace resolvأ­a el proyecto con `activeProjects().find((p) => p.name === slug)` â€”
contra el nombre CRUDO ("Pandacorp (Mission Control)")â€”, pero el dashboard/portafolio (Cartera) generan el
href con un slug **kebab** (`nameToSlug` â†’ "pandacorp-mission-control"). Nunca coincidأ­an â†’ **404 en todo el
workspace de proyecto** (Party, Observabilidad, Documentos, etc.). Se extrajo `nameToSlug` a un helper
compartido (`src/lib/slug.ts`, un solo origen â€” DR-092) y la pأ،gina ahora resuelve por slug
(`nameToSlug(p.name) === slug`), tolerando ademأ،s el nombre crudo para enlaces directos antiguos.
**Why:** Bug descubierto al intentar mostrar el Party: el deep-link estaba roto en main (el dueأ±o veأ­a una
pestaأ±a vieja en cachأ©; un refresh daba 404). El generador de enlaces y el resolutor deben compartir la
MISMA transformaciأ³n nombreâ†’slug o todo deep-link 404ea. Hueco de cobertura: el Preview Smoke Gate cubre
`/board`, `/portfolio`, `/achievements`, `/manual` pero **no** `/projects/[slug]` con un slug real, por eso
pasأ³ todos los gates estأ،ticos con la pantalla en 404.
**Context:** Test unitario de `nameToSlug` (incluye el caso exacto que rompأ­a). Fix de correctitud, separado
de la animaciأ³n del Party (REQ-06-018). Pendiente sugerido: aأ±adir el deep-link de proyecto al smoke gate.
**Impact:** Cأ³digo: `src/lib/slug.ts` (NUEVO), `src/app/projects/[slug]/page.tsx`. Tests: `src/lib/_tests/slug.test.ts` (NUEVO).

## 2026-06-29 â€” Party (La Fragua): liveness continua â€” la escena se ve VIVA entre eventos (REQ-06-018)
**What:** Nueva REQ-06-018 + implementaciأ³n. El Party se veأ­a **estأ،tico/muerto** durante builds reales: se
alimenta solo del stream de eventos de Claude Code y solo se movأ­a en las *transiciones* entre eventos, asأ­ que
con un agente moliendo una sola WO ~9 min sin eventos el muأ±equito llegaba a su hueco y se congelaba. Diagnأ³stico
a nivel de cأ³digo: los sprites se renderizan estأ،ticos desde el snapshot en posiciones fijas y el motor RAF
(`engine.tick`) se ejecutaba pero **su salida nunca se volcaba al DOM** â†’ nada animaba; ademأ،s el "halo pulsante"
del contrato de diseأ±o de `AgentSprite` **nunca se implementأ³** (solo opacidad fija) y la barra recibأ­a `progress=0`
sin fuente. Se aأ±adiأ³ **animaciأ³n ambiente continua por CSS** (no dependiente de eventos): bob + halo pulsante en
sprites en estado `work`/`review` (reusa el keyframe `campaign-idle-bob`), barra **indeterminada honesta** (sweep,
sin inventar %), **latido global "forjando en vivo / sin seأ±al reciente / en espera"** derivado de `active` +
frescura real de `lastEventAt` (umbral 4 min), y un **pulso suave en el beat activo** de la FlowStrip. Todo se
auto-desactiva con `prefers-reduced-motion` (regla global de `globals.css`) cayendo a un estado estأ،tico visible
(coherente con AC-06-014.1). **No** se inventa progreso ni datos (DR-078/087): la barra indeterminada es una seأ±al
de actividad, no un porcentaje.
**Why:** El dueأ±o reportأ³ (dos veces, mirando `:1987`) que "no se mueve nada, se ve sأ؛per estأ،tico": muأ±equitos
quietos, barra que nunca sube, y un sprite que aparecأ­a/desaparecأ­a. La causa raأ­z es de diseأ±o (visualizaciأ³n
100% event-driven sin seأ±al de vida ambiente) + dos defectos (halo no implementado, barra sin fuente). Una vista
de "vida" no puede depender solo de eventos discretos. Construido directo (el dueأ±o eligiأ³ "arreglarlo ya"),
aislado en worktree para no chocar con el build de FRD-09/10 en curso (DR-096).
**Context:** TDD â€” tests de las clases de animaciأ³n (AgentSprite, FlowStrip), `deriveHeartbeat` como funciأ³n pura,
y la transiciأ³n vivoâ†’stale con fake timers; se actualizأ³ el test adversarial `frd13-wo07-09.reviewer2` que
codificaba el comportamiento viejo (progress=0 â†’ fill 0%) al nuevo (indeterminado). Gate completo verde
(vitest 7147 + tsc/knip/biome + e2e/visual 56). Queda **pendiente** (capturado en la change-card
`mc-party-liveness-heartbeat.md`): arreglar de raأ­z el **parpadeo** aparecer/desaparecer (la presencia del sprite

## 2026-06-29 â€” WO-09-006: gamification ledger â€” persistent XP accumulator
**What:** Implemented the gamification ledger (`factory/gamification-ledger.json`, gitignored) that
records the historical maximum guild outcomes (workOrdersDone, phasesCompleted, releases) so that
deleting a project NEVER decreases the guild's XP or level. Three new artifacts: (1)
`lib/gamification/ledger.ts` â€” pure module with `readLedger` (DR-078 compliant: never throws,
zero-totals on absent/malformed), `mergeLedgerOutcomes` (MAX(live, ledger) per metric), and
`needsSnapshot` (detects when a write is needed); (2) `app/_actions/snapshotLedger.ts` â€” Server
Action that reads, compares, and writes the ledger only when needsSnapshot is true (fire-and-forget,
never blocks render); (3) `GamificationLedgerSync` client component (renders null) mounted in
`app/page.tsx` â€” calls the action once after hydration. Integration: the ledger merge now happens
inside `readGuildState()` in `lib/gamification/guildState.ts` (the single source of truth) so all
three surfaces (GuildBar, dashboard, Logros hero) pick up the ledger floor at once. `GuildState`
exposes both `liveOutcomes` (pre-merge, for the snapshot action) and `outcomes` (post-merge, for the
level computation). `factory/gamification-ledger.json` added to the factory root `.gitignore`.
**Why:** AC-09-006.1â€“3 (FRD-09). Ensures historical XP is never lost when a project is deleted.
The write is fire-and-forget (never blocks TTFB). Personal data â€” gitignored (DR-033).
**Impact:** `docs/frds/frd-09-gamification/frd.md` (AC-09-006 already present); `docs/design/components.md`
(new `GamificationLedgerSync` row); `.gitignore` (ledger entry); `lib/gamification/guildState.ts`
(ledger merge integrated into single source of truth).

## 2026-06-29 â€” Fix: la escalera de nodos de las misiones no dibujaba el primer tramo (FRD-10)
**What:** En `ChainCard` (`NodeLadder`), la lأ­nea conectora entre el **punto 1 y el punto 2** no aparecأ­a â€” el primer punto quedaba suelto a la izquierda con un hueco. Fix: el `<span>` del nodo 0 ya no usa `flex: 1` sino `flex: 0 0 auto`, asأ­ no deja espacio vacأ­o a su derecha y el conector del nodo 1 (que vive en el span del nodo 1) cubre el primer hueco completo.
**Why:** Cada nodo se envolvأ­a en un `<span flex:1>` con `(conector si i>0) + punto`. **Context:** Bug reportado por el dueأ±o al revisar la pأ،gina de logros. ## 2026-06-29 â€” Salأ³n de Logros v2 ("la pأ،gina أ©pica"): catأ،logo enorme + re-anclaje a eventos REALES (FRD-10)
**What:** Ampliaciأ³n del Salأ³n de Logros de 15 trofeos / 12 cadenas / 3 secretos a **~80 trofeos en 8 ejes**, **~21 cadenas agrupadas en sagas** y **~18 secretos**, con **rareza por trofeo** (Comأ؛nâ†’Leyenda, pirأ،mide â‰ˆ40/25/17/11/6%), **Sellos** (meta-logro por completar un eje, + Gran Sello), badge **NUEVO** (7 dأ­as) y rareza estimada. Dos ejes nuevos de categorأ­a (Producciأ³n, Gremio, Temple, sumados a Discovery/Speed/Quality/Consistency/Mastery). El catأ،logo completo, el mapa de seأ±ales y el modelo de rareza viven en `docs/achievements.md` v2.
**Why (hallazgo crأ­tico):** El dueأ±o pidiأ³ "muchos mأ،s logros y misiones, que se sienta una app rica". Investigando se descubriأ³ que el problema no era solo el conteo: **la mayorأ­a de los predicados v1 leأ­an un evento `"achievement"` con `task="prd"/"adr"/"flawless"/"iteration"/"speed:N"/"phase:X"/"release"` que NADIE emite** â€” no existe en ningأ؛n `emit-event` del plugin. El stream real (`~/.claude/dashboard-events.ndjson`, ~4300 eventos) contiene `SubagentStop`, `AgentWorking`, `SupervisorTick`, `ReviewVerdict`, `GateVerdict`, `GateResult`, `BuildLaunch/Complete/Relaunch`, `AgentDone`, `AgentFinding` (con `data.{role,wo,verdict,result,reopen_count,blocking,important,mode,maxAgents,effort,â€¦}`). Por eso ~9 de 15 trofeos estaban **dormidos para siempre** y la pأ،gina se sentأ­a vacأ­a aunque hubiera muchأ­simo trabajo real hecho. v2 **re-ancla cada desbloqueo a esa seأ±al real** para que los logros se enciendan de verdad.
**Context:** Decisiأ³n del dueأ±o (deep-research â†’ iterate): alcance "catأ،logo + cablear seأ±ales reales", volumen "enorme". Restricciأ³n dura del contrato de honestidad: ningأ؛n logro sin seأ±al real verificable (los evocativos sin seأ±al van a `docs/achievements.md` آ§8 "pending emitter", nunca como trofeo dormido). Requiere extender `lib/events/events.ts` para exponer los campos enriquecidos reales (`verdict`, `result`, `reopenCount`, `blocking`, `important`, `agentType`, `effort`, `maxAgents`, `wos`/`frds`, `reason`) con **parseo fail-loud** (DR-078), y que el motor de logros lea el stream **sin cap** (los contadores que solo crecen no deben "des-desbloquearse" al crecer el tail de 200). Sin cambio de estأ©tica (a pedido): es ampliaciأ³n de contenido + cableado, no rediseأ±o visual.
**Impact:** Canأ³nico: `docs/achievements.md` (reescrito a v2 â€” آ§1 vocabulario de seأ±ales reales, آ§2 rareza+Sellos, آ§3 los 8 ejes, آ§4 Sellos, آ§5 ~18 secretos con pista, آ§6 sagas, آ§8 pending-emitter) + `docs/frds/frd-10-achievements-hall/frd.md` (secciأ³n v2 + ACs nuevas: rareza por trofeo, 8 ejes, Sellos, NUEVO, sagas, honestidad/fail-loud). ## 2026-06-29 â€” La Campaأ±a: roam ambiente â€” los muأ±equitos se mueven en CUALQUIER fase, no solo en el build (REQ-02-010)
**What:** En La Campaأ±a (tab Campaأ±a del detalle de tarjeta, `CampaignPipeline`/`RoamingCast`), el cast de la **fase activa** ahora **siempre roamea** (vaga) como tema visual de "aquأ­ estأ، la idea ahora", para **cualquier** fase (researchâ†’release), **desacoplado** del flag `running`. Antes el roam exigأ­a `running===true`, y `running:true` lo pone **exclusivamente** `/pandacorp:implement` (el supervisor del build) â€” por eso solo la sala de construcciأ³n se animaba y las de design/spec/blueprint quedaban congeladas (idle-bob). El **split honesto** se preserva: el **halo** del lأ­der y los **bocadillos al encontrarse** (speech-on-meet) siguen apareciendo **solo** con un agente realmente corriendo (`running`), y la etiqueta de la ficha/badge ("fase actual" vs "â—ڈ en curso") **no cambia** â€” asأ­ el movimiento es ambiente pero no se fabrica actividad de trabajo real.
**Why:** Pedido del dueأ±o: al seguir un proyecto en el tablero (p.ej. PersonalPage v2 en fase design), no veأ­a moverse los muأ±equitos aunque se estaba trabajando esa secciأ³n; querأ­a que la Campaأ±a "cobre vida" en la fase activa. Investigado: la causa era el gate `state==='current' && running` y que `running` es solo del build. Decisiأ³n (opciأ³n "Ambiente"): movimiento ambiente en la fase activa, manteniendo honestos la etiqueta y los marcadores de trabajo real.
**Context:** Cambio **100% Mission Control** â€” no toca ningأ؛n skill, agente ni hook. Una decisiأ³n de una lأ­nea en el effect de roam (`RoamingCast.tsx:99`: quitar `|| !running`) + los bocadillos atados a `running` dentro de `arrive()` (asأ­ `running` sigue justificado en el dep array y Biome queda limpio). El halo y el span de speech ya estaban condicionados a `running` en el JSX. Implementado por `/pandacorp:iterate` con TDD (test guardrail: el halo solo aparece con `running`). El roam en sأ­ es imperativo por RAF (no se asserta en jsdom); se verifica en el navegador.
**Impact:** Canأ³nico: `docs/frds/frd-02-ideas-board/frd.md` (enmienda de la AC de liveliness de REQ-02-010, 2026-06-29). Cأ³digo: `src/components/modules/CampaignPipeline/RoamingCast.tsx` (roam desacoplado de `running`; speech gated en `arrive`). Tests: `CampaignPipeline.test.tsx` (+2: halo ausente sin `running`, presente con `running`). WO: `wo-02-007-card-detail.md` reabierto (Status Note 2026-06-29) â†’ VERIFIED al pasar el gate.

## 2026-06-28 â€” Favoritos en el tablero: marcar ideas/proyectos como favoritos (solo visual, cualquier columna) â€” REQ-02-012, ADR-0003
**What:** Nueva funcionalidad en el board: el dueأ±o puede **marcar una tarjeta como favorita** con una **estrella** (toggle) en la esquina superior derecha de cualquier card (cualquier columna) y tambiأ©n en el header del detalle. UI optimista (`useOptimistic`). La estrella es el control **y** el indicador no-cromأ،tico (forma + `aria-pressed`), reforzado por `aria-label` "(favorita)" â€” nunca solo color.
**Why:** Pedido del dueأ±o: poder identificar de un vistazo las ideas/proyectos que le importan, sin tocar el pipeline. "Que su fondo del card sea de otro color, acorde al diseأ±o" â†’ se eligiأ³ el dorado (estrella = convenciأ³n universal de favorito) por ser semأ،nticamente "destacado" y distinto de los acentos ya usados.

**Impact:** Canأ³nico: `frd-02-ideas-board/frd.md` (REQ-02-012 + edge case), su `blueprint.md` (CMP-02-favorite/-action, IF-02-setFavorite, آ§3 writes acotados, traza), `fdd.md` (آ§10 highlight dorado + estrella), `work-orders/{README.md,wo-02-012-favorite.md}`, `docs/design/components.md` (fila FavoriteButton), `docs/product/architecture.md` (آ§1/آ§4 campo `favorite`/آ§6/آ§7 writes acotados), **ADR-0003** (nuevo). ## 2026-06-27 â€” Spec tab: render mأ،s escaneable (problemaâ†’bullets, hipأ³tesisâ†’callout, alcanceâ†’checklist, sin tachado) (AC-02-011.2)
**What:** Mejora del render del tab Spec (`SpecDigest`) tras feedback del owner: la **hipأ³tesis** dejaba un muro de texto, **usuarios/mأ©tricas** salأ­an desordenadas (puro tأ­tulo, sin descripciأ³n), el **alcance** se veأ­a apretado y **fuera del v1** tenأ­a un **tachado** ilegible. Ahora: **El problema** â†’ lista de bullets (va primero, es el punto de partida); **Hipأ³tesis de valor** â†’ un callout destacado corto; **Usuarios/Mأ©tricas** â†’ cards tأ­tulo+descripciأ³n; **Alcance** â†’ checklist holgado (no pills); **Fuera del v1** â†’ chips apagados **sin tachado**. Dos kinds nuevos en el parser (`bullets`, `highlight`) + el orden lo decide el digest.
**Why:** El bug raأ­z: el regex del parser exigأ­a el guion *justo* tras el `**tأ­tulo**`; con un parأ©ntesis en medio (`- **Rol** (x) â€” desc`) no matcheaba â†’ caأ­a a "plano" â†’ el tأ­tulo se tragaba toda la lأ­nea y la descripciأ³n quedaba vacأ­a (por eso usuarios/mأ©tricas salأ­an como "puro tأ­tulo"). Se hizo el parser **tolerante** (tأ­tulo = el `**bold**`, desc = el resto), asأ­ un bullet mal autorado igual rinde tأ­tulo+descripciأ³n. Y se ajustأ³ el formato/template para que la prأ³xima pasada del skill lo genere bien.
**Context:** Verificado en vivo (board â†’ PersonalPage v2 â†’ Spec): problema 4 bullets, hipأ³tesis callout, 3 role cards, 5 stat cards TODAS con descripciأ³n, 10 أ­tems de checklist, fuera `text-decoration: none`.
**Impact:** Canأ³nico: `docs/frds/frd-02-ideas-board/frd.md` (AC-02-011.2 reescrito). Cأ³digo: `lib/spec/spec.ts` (parser tolerante + kinds `bullets`/`highlight`), `SpecDigest/SpecDigest.tsx` + `.styles.ts` (componentes Highlight/BulletList/ScopeList; quitado el tachado). Tests: `spec.test.ts` + `SpecDigest.test.tsx` (+cobertura de los kinds nuevos). Plantilla del skill: `plugin/templates/docs/spec-digest-template.md` (orden problema-primero + reglas de autorأ­a de las cards) â€” plugin 9.22.0â†’9.22.1.

## 2026-06-27 â€” Hint en el spec de Producto + fix de test flaky (CardDetail in-doc-link)
**What (tema 3):** El comando `spec` de la fase **Producto** ("Pule el PRD/FRDs") no tenأ­a `hint`, asأ­ que en `default` no mostraba lأ­nea de ayuda (el de **research** sأ­). Se le aأ±ade el mismo hint para que ambas fichas se comporten igual (conforme a AC-02-010.9, que ya exige el hint del modo/ default). **What (flaky):** El test `frd-02: an external in-doc link stays a new-tab anchor` (`CardDetail.test.tsx`) fallaba intermitentemente SOLO en el gate completo (no aislado: 6/6 con shuffle). Causa: el `waitFor` de `openPrd` (default 1s) se quedaba corto bajo la carga paralela de 345 archivos (el body del PRD se fetchea+parsea async). Fix: `timeout: 4000` + queries scoped al `container` del render (en vez de `screen` global) para blindar contra cualquier nodo stale.
**Why:** Consistencia de la ficha (tema 3) y eliminar el ruido del flake (un test que falla a veces erosiona la confianza en el gate; DR de test discipline: pasa aislado Y en cualquier orden).
**Impact:** Cأ³digo: `CampaignPipeline/phases.ts` (hint del spec de producto), `CardDetail/_tests/CardDetail.test.tsx` (`within(container)` + `timeout`). Sin cambio de comportamiento de app fuera del hint. Verificado: CardDetail 54/54 en 4 shuffles + gate completo.

## 2026-06-27 â€” Tooltip propio del select: arriba, instantأ،neo, ancho acotado (AC-02-010.9)
**What:** El tooltip del campo usaba el atributo `title` nativo â†’ lento (delay del navegador), posicionado abajo y sin ancho mأ،ximo. Se reemplaza por un **tooltip propio** en `CmdRow`: aparece **arriba** del select, **al instante** en hover/focus (state-driven, sin delay), con **max-width ~240px** y wrap a 2-3 lأ­neas, estilado con tokens. Se quita el `title` nativo (evita el doble tooltip) y el texto se cablea como `aria-describedby` (role="tooltip") para lectores de pantalla.
**Why:** El owner pidiأ³ que el tooltip salga arriba, inmediato y con ancho delimitado â€” nada de eso es posible con el `title` nativo (el navegador lo controla). Un tooltip propio da control total de posiciأ³n, timing y ancho.
**Context:** Implementado con `useState` (tipOpen) + `useId` en `CmdRow` (ya es "use client"); el `<select>` se envuelve en un `span` position:relative que ancla el bubble (bottom: calc(100%+6px), right:0 para no desbordar el borde derecho de la fila). `pointer-events:none` en el bubble. Verificado en vivo: arriba âœ“, 240px âœ“, ~3 lأ­neas âœ“, instantأ،neo âœ“.
**Impact:** Canأ³nico: `docs/frds/frd-02-ideas-board/frd.md` (AC-02-010.9: tooltip propio en vez de `title`). Cأ³digo: `components/core/CmdRow/CmdRow.tsx` (tooltip custom + `aria-describedby`; sin `title`). Tests: el test de tooltip pasa de comprobar `title` a comprobar el bubble en hover + `aria-describedby`.

## 2026-06-27 â€” Select de modo: la opciأ³n default es `default` (neutro), el campo va al tooltip (AC-02-010.9)
**What:** Corrige la iteraciأ³n anterior. Ahora la primera opciأ³n es la palabra neutra **`default`** ("sin flag, el skill decide") para ambos comandos; **quأ© controla el campo** lo lleva el **tooltip** (con mأ،s contexto: spec â†’ "Cuأ،ntas preguntas te hago antes de generar la documentaciأ³n"; implement â†’ "Modo de construcciأ³n â€” con cuأ،nta potencia se construye el proyecto") + la lأ­nea de hint. Mأ،s angosto aأ؛n (spec ~89px) y sin la ambigأ¼edad.
**Why:** El owner seأ±alأ³ el conflicto semأ،ntico: la etiqueta-opciأ³n no puede ser a la vez "el nombre del campo" y "el valor elegido". `default` separa ambos: la opciأ³n dice claramente "no he elegido flag", y el tooltip/hint dan el contexto del campo (y caben con mأ،s detalle que en una opciأ³n de select).
**Impact:** Canأ³nico: `docs/frds/frd-02-ideas-board/frd.md` (AC-02-010.9: opciأ³n default = `default` + tooltip con contexto). Cأ³digo: `lib/command-modes.ts` (`SPEC/IMPLEMENT_MODE_DEFAULT_LABEL = "default"`; `*_MODE_TITLE` mأ،s descriptivos). Tests: aserciones de etiqueta a `default`. ## 2026-06-27 â€” Select de modo: etiqueta default a UNA palabra + tooltip (mأ،s angosto) (AC-02-010.9)
**What:** La primera opciأ³n ("sin flag") del select dejaba de caber: cargaba categorأ­a + "es el default" en un texto largo (`preguntas: default` / `modo: equilibrado`), y como el ancho del `<select>` nativo lo manda la opciأ³n mأ،s larga, el control salأ­a ancho. Ahora la opciأ³n default es **una sola palabra** que nombra el campo: `preguntas` (spec) / `Equilibrado` (implement). El nombre completo del campo va al **tooltip** (`title` del select, prop nuevo `modeTitle` en `CmdRow`) y el detalle sigue en la **lأ­nea de hint**. Resultado: el select del spec baja de ~150px a **~104px**, y escala sin ensancharse con 2-3+ opciones.
**Why:** El owner notأ³ que `preguntas: default` hacأ­a el select demasiado ancho (mismo problema de espacio que las pأ­ldoras). Mover la categorأ­a a la palabra-opciأ³n + el resto al hint/tooltip mantiene los tres requisitos (saber quأ© campo es آ· quأ© opciأ³n elegأ­ آ· quأ© hace) sin gastar ancho.
**Impact:** Canأ³nico: `docs/frds/frd-02-ideas-board/frd.md` (AC-02-010.9: opciأ³n default = palabra corta + tooltip). Cأ³digo: `lib/command-modes.ts` (`SPEC/IMPLEMENT_MODE_DEFAULT_LABEL` acortados + `*_MODE_TITLE` nuevos), `CmdRow.tsx` (prop `modeTitle`â†’`title`), `phases.ts`/`CampaignPipeline.tsx`/`mode-selector.tsx` (pasan `modeTitle`). Tests: aserciones de etiqueta actualizadas + test del tooltip. Verificado en vivo (104px, opciones cortas, tooltip presente).

## 2026-06-27 â€” FRD-11 al `<select>` compacto + mأ³dulo compartido `command-modes` (DR-092)
**What:** El selector de build mode del **tab Comandos del portafolio** (FRD-11) pasa de su **panel de 4 chips radio** (fidelity-tested al prototipo) a la **misma fila CmdRow con `<select>` compacto** del tablero. ## 2026-06-27 â€” FRD-21: indicador global de "pendientes de merge" en el shell (DR-096, construido)

## 2026-06-26 â€” Descarte: reusar el Button core (variante danger) + fix de hover + textarea grande/ilimitado (FRD-02/FRD-13, DR-057)
**What:** Tres arreglos al flujo de descarte, todos pedidos por el owner:
- **Reuso del `Button` core (DR-057):** el `DiscardButton` se inventaba sus propios estilos de botأ³n a mano (`BASE/DISCARD/CONFIRM/CANCEL_BTN_STYLE`). Ahora los **tres** botones (trigger, "Sأ­, descartar", "Cancelar") son el `Button` compartido â€” *el mismo componente, distintos estilos*, como pedأ­a el owner. Se aأ±adiأ³ al `Button` una prop **`tone` (default/danger)** que se compone con `variant`: `secondary`+`danger` = **outline rojo** (el trigger), `primary`+`danger` = **relleno rojo** (confirmar), `secondary` default = "Cancelar". El `Button` emite `data-tone` para que el CSS apunte el hover correcto.
- **Fix del hover ilegible:** el botأ³n relleno "Sأ­, descartar" en hover cambiaba su fondo rojo sأ³lido por el tinte oscuro `--color-danger-bg`, dejando el texto `--color-on-accent` (casi negro en oscuro) sobre fondo oscuro â†’ ilegible. Nuevo hover **consciente del tono** en `globals.css`: el relleno (`[data-tone=danger][data-variant=primary]:hover`) **mantiene fondo sأ³lido** (apenas profundizado con `color-mix`) + glow; el outline tinta suave. El hover accent base se acota con `:not([data-tone="danger"])`. Contraste verificado en claro y oscuro (el token `on-accent` se voltea por tema: texto oscuro sobre rojo claro / texto blanco sobre rojo oscuro).
- **Textarea del motivo:** `minHeight` 52â†’**140px**, fuente 12â†’13px, ancho completo (se quitأ³ el `maxWidth:360` del form), y **se eliminأ³ `maxLength={280}`** â€” acepta cualquier cantidad de texto (el owner no le veأ­a sentido al lأ­mite).
**Why:** El owner notأ³ que el botأ³n de descartar y el de confirmar se veأ­an distintos sin ser el mismo componente (intuiciأ³n correcta: era una violaciأ³n de reuso DR-057), que el hover "se ve horrible" (texto negro ilegible) y que el textarea era muy pequeأ±o y con lأ­mite arbitrario. Implementado vأ­a `/pandacorp:iterate`.
**Verified:** TDD â€” `Button` 5 tests nuevos de `tone` (default/danger, filled vs outline) + `DiscardButton` 30/30. **Button+DiscardButton+board 377/377** verdes; gate completo `verify.sh` **exit 0** (incluye e2e visual â€” sin cambios de baseline: el trigger no estأ، en ningأ؛n baseline y el resto de Buttons no cambian su estado en reposo). **Navegador en vivo** (`localhost:3000`, modal de descarte): los 4 botones son `.pc-btn`; confirm = `data-tone=danger`/`variant=primary` fondo rojo sأ³lido, trigger = outline, cancel = secondary; hover relleno resuelve a fondo sأ³lido `rgb(211,88,77)` (no tinte); textarea 140px sin `maxlength`; verificado en claro y oscuro.
**Impact:** `src/components/core/Button/Button.tsx` (prop `tone` + `variantStyle(variant, tone)` + `data-tone`) + sus tests; `src/app/globals.css` (hover por tono; eliminada `.pc-discard:hover`); `src/components/core/DiscardButton/DiscardButton.tsx` (usa `Button`, eliminados los estilos a mano, textarea agrandado sin lأ­mite). Doc canأ³nico: `docs/design/components.md` (fila `Button` â†’ variante `tone`/danger, DR-057). El contrato de FRD-02 (descartar con motivo) no cambia; es presentaciأ³n + reuso.

## 2026-06-26 â€” Descarte de idea: captura del motivo en MODAL, no inline (FRD-02, REQ-02-007)
**What:** Al pulsar **"Descartar idea"** en el detalle de una card, el formulario de motivo (quick-tags + texto libre + confirmar/cancelar) ya **no se expande inline** empujando el contenido hacia abajo: ahora abre el **`Modal` compartido** (`components/core/Modal/Modal.tsx`, DR-057) â€” el mismo primitive que usan la captura de ideas (IntakeModal) y "Ver descartadas" (DiscardedModal). El `DiscardButton` mantiene su trigger **siempre montado** (sin salto de layout) y conmuta el modal con su mأ،quina de estados existente (`idle â†’ confirming â†’ pending â†’ done`); mientras el write estأ، en vuelo el modal queda abierto con "Descartandoâ€¦" deshabilitado y **backdrop/âœ•/Escape son inertes** hasta que se resuelve (no se puede abandonar un write destructivo a medias). El comportamiento de captura (tags multi-select + texto, composiciأ³n del `discard_reason`, optimistic UI, errores) es idأ©ntico â€” solo cambia la presentaciأ³n.
**Why:** El owner reportأ³ que el descarte inline "se ve horrible" y pidiأ³ moverlo a un modal reutilizando el `Modal` existente. Esto ademأ،s **alinea el descarte con la propia regla del owner ya escrita en el FRD-02** ("reveal-more is a modal, never an inline expand-that-pushes-content") y en el docstring del `Modal` â€” la captura del motivo era la أ؛ltima superficie que la violaba. ## 2026-06-26 â€” FRD-20: indicador de "frescura de overlay" en el Resumen del proyecto (آ؟desfasado de la fأ،brica?)
**What:** Nuevo **FRD-20 â€” Project overlay freshness**. ## 2026-06-25 â€” Descartar captura el PORQUأ‰: `discard_reason` (FRD-02, AC-02-007.2)
**What:** Al descartar una idea, el flujo de confirmaciأ³n de `DiscardButton` ahora ofrece capturar **un motivo opcional** â€” quick-tags (saturado/competencia آ· no me interesa el tema آ· no apalanca mi canal آ· muy complejo آ· no monetiza en Perأ؛ آ· otro) + texto libre â€” y lo escribe en el campo `discard_reason` del frontmatter, junto a `status: discarded`, **en la misma أ؛nica escritura** (`lib/discard/discard.ts` ahora acepta un 3er parأ،metro `reason`; `discardIdeaAction` lo propaga). El motivo es opcional: confirmar sin elegir nada escribe solo `status` (comportamiento previo, byte-clean). Verificado con TDD (95 tests del flujo de descarte + 6938 de la suite, gate verde) y en el navegador (el formulario aparece al confirmar, sin errores de consola; cancelar no descarta).
**Why:** El owner pidiأ³ cerrar el loop de feedback de descartes â€” *"yo descarto una idea, pero آ؟hay forma de que recibas el porquأ© y no me recomiendes cosas con ese mismo patrأ³n? De ser posible dentro de la app."* El lado fأ،brica ya estaba (discover lee `discard_reason` y aprende patrones de rechazo, plugin v9.8.0); faltaba la **captura en la app**. Antes, descartar escribأ­a solo `status` sin pedir motivo (por eso el owner no veأ­a ninguna opciأ³n). Implementado directo por indicaciأ³n explأ­cita del owner (normalmente irأ­a por `/pandacorp:iterate`; se mantuvo el rigor: TDD + FRD + este log).
**Impact:** `src/lib/discard/discard.ts` (3er arg `reason` â†’ `discard_reason`), `src/app/board/actions/actions.ts` (propaga), `src/components/core/DiscardButton/DiscardButton.tsx` (formulario de motivo en el paso de confirmaciأ³n), `src/app/board/_components/BoardShell/BoardShell.tsx` (tipo del prop). ## 2026-06-25 â€” Sistema de rangos: nivel granular + rango por BANDA de niveles + grado romano (Fase 5)

## 2026-06-25 â€” Gate visual: enmascarar las listas de datos vivos con `data-volatile` (DR-088)
**What:** El gate de fidelidad visual (`e2e/visual.spec.ts`, `toHaveScreenshot({fullPage:true})`) fallaba en falso en `/board` (tablero) y `/proposals` (propuestas): ambos baselines estaban acoplados a **datos vivos de la fأ،brica** (las tarjetas de idea del tablero; los cuatro streams de auto-aprendizaje + la cola de promociones de propuestas) mأ،s un reflow cold/warm, asأ­ que la altura de pأ،gina derivaba (propuestas 9769â†’9986â†’10203px en una sola sesiأ³n; el tablero en cada alta/descarte/ediciأ³n de tarjeta) y el snapshot no calzaba aunque la ruta renderizara bien. ## 2026-06-25 â€” FRD-09: gamification ledger (persistent XP accumulator) â€” WO-09-006 added
**What:** Added WO-09-006 to FRD-09 with a new `lib/gamification/ledger.ts` module, a Server Action `snapshotLedger`, and a `GamificationLedgerSync` client component. The ledger (`factory/gamification-ledger.json`, gitignored) stores the maximum guild outcomes ever seen (workOrdersDone, phasesCompleted, releases); the dashboard merges `MAX(live, ledger)` so that deleting a project never decreases the guild's XP or level.
**Why:** Today `deriveGuildOutcomes` derives everything from live `status.yaml` files. If a project is deleted, its contribution vanishes and the guild loses level/XP. The owner identified this as a broken invariant â€” achievements should be cumulative and permanent. The ledger is a "snapshot-on-exceed" pattern: whenever live > stored, MC updates the file; if a project later disappears, the historical max persists.
**Impact:** `docs/frds/frd-09-gamification/frd.md` (+AC-09-006.1/2/3), `blueprint.md` (آ§5 posture + Build Plan Phase 3), `work-orders/wo-09-006-gamification-ledger.md` (new), `work-orders/README.md` (new row). `status.yaml`: `work_orders_total` 79â†’80, `work_orders_planned` 0â†’1. `/implement` will build WO-09-006 on its next run (independent of WO-09-003).

## 2026-06-24 â€” Observabilidad DAG: 2D compound (cluster) layout is now official + the WO dependency map written to the frontmatter
**What:** Two coupled changes. (1) **The DAG view is now a 2D compound layout** (replacing the 1D swimlanes): each FRD is an opaque box placed in free 2D by a **deterministic seeded force sim + AABB no-overlap pass**; WO cards inside (2-line); intra-FRD WOâ†’WO lines on top, cross-FRD lines **aggregated to one FRDâ†’FRD line per pair** drawn behind the boxes; **color-on-select** (click pins a card â†’ its intra chain + immediate FRD neighbors recolor with distinct `--color-trace-N` tokens, the rest dims). Layout is computed from STRUCTURE ONLY and is byte-deterministic, so live state changes only recolor cards â€” boxes never jump (this is how the force layout the red-team flagged for non-determinism is made safe). (2) **The full audited dependency map (244 deps) was written to the WO `dependsOn` frontmatter** â€” until now the frontmatter only had a sparse README-derived backfill (5 cross-FRD pairs), so the real DAG looked disconnected; now it shows the real graph (58 FRDâ†”FRD links, hubs FRD-13/FRD-01 central).
**Why:** Owner adopted 2D after iterating on the prototype `docs/design/prototype/dag-2d.html` (he validated the look, the FRD-aggregated cross lines, the color-on-select tracing, no-overlap, 2-line cards). The map came from the 3-agent evidence-based audit (real source imports): it confirmed the couplings he flagged (partyâ†گbuild-modes, achievementsâ†گgamification+events, every UI surfaceâ†گFRD-13 foundations, the dashboard depends on ~half the system). Overrides the earlier red-team default (1D swimlanes) because the owner saw 2D and prefers it, and the determinism objection is resolved (seeded + structural-only). Rejected the iframe-to-static-HTML idea (frozen MC-only data, no live, no per-project) â€” ported into the real React `WoDag` instead.
**Verified:** `verify.sh` GREEN (328 test files, 6917 tests + 2 xfail; smoke/visual/responsive/shell); new layout/highlight tests (deterministic same-inputâ†’same-output, no cluster overlap, aggregated cross, color-on-select). Live (dev :3000): MC DAG renders 19 cluster boxes, 79 cards, 58 cross lines, 244 deps; click WO-09-003 â†’ 8 distinct trace colors + 39 cards dimmed; zero console errors.
**Impact:** New `_observability/WoDag/{forceLayout,deps,highlight,DagCanvas,DagCard,Legend,Controls}.tsx/.ts` + rewritten `layout.ts`/`WoDag.tsx` (deleted `DagNodeGroup.tsx`); `globals.css` + `docs/design/design-tokens.json` (+`--color-trace-1..10`); 53 WO `dependsOn` frontmatters; prototype archived at `docs/design/prototype/dag-2d.html` (+generator). Canonical: **FRD-12 AC-12-004.1/.1b/.2**. Manual: `concepts/mission-control-por-dentro`. NOTE: the work-orders README "Depends on" columns now lag the (authoritative) frontmatter â€” a separate reconcile task is flagged. MC-only â€” no factory/plugin change (the `dependsOn` contract shipped earlier under DR-087).

## 2026-06-24 â€” Observabilidad DAG: order swimlanes by FRD-dependency (related FRDs adjacent) â€” red-team rejected force-directed/Obsidian
**What:** The FRD swimlanes were stacked by FRD **number**; now they're ordered by **FRD-level dependency** so related FRDs sit adjacent. `orderedFrdGroups` builds the FRD super-graph (a cross-FRD WO edge Aâ†’B â‡’ FRD(A)â†’FRD(B)) and emits a **DFS pre-order from the prerequisite roots** (each dependency chain contiguous; a prerequisite FRD immediately followed by its dependents), numeric-FRD tie-break, cycle-safe fallback. Result: FRD-18 (depends on FRD-01) now lands directly under FRD-01 with a short dashed edge instead of 17 bands away.
**Why:** Owner: with FRD swimlanes the graph was still "desordenado" and related FRDs were far apart; he asked whether related FRDs should sit near each other in 2D (Obsidian-style). Ran a **6-agent red-team** (3 option-advocates + 2 skeptics + judge, high confidence): **force-directed/Obsidian REJECTED** â€” non-deterministic across server reads + live updates (nodes jitter), and it destroys the directional/topological reading (what-blocks-what, chain-highlight, jump-to-first-error) that is FRD-12's core value, plus a new dep. Winner: **swimlanes ordered by dependency** (deterministic, no new dep, keeps direction, ~80% of the intent). True 2D (compound-nested-layered) is the deferred phase-2 if 1D adjacency proves insufficient. I implemented the DFS-contiguous variant (over the judge's rank-based spec) because it best delivers the owner's literal example (FRD-18 adjacent to FRD-01).
**Verified:** `verify.sh` GREEN (327 files, 6917 tests + 2 xfail); live (fresh dev server, no HMR) DAG bands order FRD-01 â†’ FRD-18 â†’ FRD-02â€¦, 19 bands, 7 dashed cross-FRD edges, zero console errors. New layout tests: prereq-before-dependent ordering (beats numeric), DFS adjacency (dependent right after its prerequisite).
**Impact:** `_observability/WoDag/layout.ts` (`orderedFrdGroups` topo/DFS order + `groupNodesByFrd`/`buildFrdSuperGraph` helpers; now takes `edges`), its tests. Canonical: **FRD-12 AC-12-004.1b**. MC-only. Deferred (phase-2, if needed): compound 2D cluster layout. Noted by the red-team for separate cleanup: `@dagrejs/dagre` + the dead `_observability/dag/WorkOrderDag` component are unused in the live path.

## 2026-06-24 â€” Observabilidad DAG: FRD swimlanes layout (ordered + grouped) instead of one global layered graph
**What:** Reworked the DAG layout from a single global topological layout into **per-FRD swimlanes**. Each FRD is a labeled horizontal band ("FRD-NN آ· Name", ordered by FRD number); within a band, its WOs are ranked left-to-right by the band's **internal** dependency depth (only intra-FRD edges). Cross-FRD edges render **dashed** to read as jumps between bands. `computeLayout` now returns `lanes[]` + `crossFrd` per edge; `DagNode` carries `frd` (set by `toDag`); the SVG draws a faint labeled band rect per lane behind the nodes.
**Why:** Owner: with real dependencies the graph "se ve demasiado desordenado" â€” the global layered layout piled every dependency-free WO into a giant rank-0 first column (45+ nodes) while later columns were tiny. Research (Sugiyama / clustered level graphs / swimlanes) + the owner's instinct both point to FRD grouping: it removes the global root pile-up (each FRD's roots pile only within its small band) and matches the mental model. Honest data unchanged (DR-087) â€” only the arrangement.
**Verified:** `verify.sh` GREEN; live (dev :3000) DAG renders 19 FRD bands (FRD-01â€¦FRD-19, labeled), 46 intra-FRD edges + 7 dashed cross-FRD edges, fan-out/fan-in visible within bands, zero console errors. New layout tests: lanes ordered by FRD number, frd-02 band below frd-01, intra-FRD column order, cross-FRD flagged.
**Impact:** `_observability/WoDag/layout.ts` (swimlane `computeLayout` + `DagLane`/`crossFrd` + lane constants), `app/_observability/dag/dag/dag.ts` (`DagNode.frd`), `_observability/WoDag/WoDag.tsx` (render lane bands + dashed cross-FRD edges), their tests. Canonical: **FRD-12 AC-12-004.1b**. MC-only â€” no factory/plugin change (the `dependsOn` data contract already shipped under DR-087).

## 2026-06-24 â€” Observabilidad DAG: real dependencies from `dependsOn` frontmatter (DR-087) â€” killed the fabricated linear chain
**What:** The dependency DAG drew a **fake linear chain** (every WO depended on exactly one other). Root cause: `lib/work-orders` read no dependencies, and `WoDag/layout.ts` `deriveDeps` **fabricated** a "depends on the previous WO in its FRD" fallback for any WO without explicit deps â€” which was all of them. Now: `lib/work-orders` reads **`dependsOn`** from the WO frontmatter (the machine-readable source, DR-087); `deriveDeps` uses it verbatim (filtered to known ids, self-refs dropped) with **no fallback** â€” a WO with no deps is an independent node. MC's 33 existing WOs were **backfilled** into `dependsOn` from each FRD's `work-orders/README.md` "Depends on" column. The DAG now shows the real graph: fan-out (WO-01-000 â†’ 7), fan-in (WO-18-001 â†گ 6 across 4 FRDs), non-sequential (WO-06-001 â†گ WO-06-012), 7 cross-FRD edges, 13 nodes with multiple incoming.
**Why:** Owner: every WO depending on exactly one other "en la vida real nunca ha sido asأ­". Investigation confirmed the real cross-deps existed (README "Depends on" column, 15/19 FRDs) but MC fabricated instead of reading them â€” the same anti-pattern as the timeline's fake bars. Owner chose deps-as-frontmatter (durable, machine-readable) over parsing the prose README at runtime.
**Verified:** `verify.sh` GREEN; live (dev :3000) DAG renders 53 edges with real fan-in/out + cross-FRD, zero console errors; new tests (deriveDeps keeps real cross/fan-in, no fabricated chain, drops dangling/self; WoDag renders real edges incl. cross-FRD, no edges when none declared).
**Impact:** `src/lib/work-orders/work-orders.ts` (parse `dependsOn`), `_observability/WoDag/layout.ts` (`deriveDeps` de-fabricated; removed the seq-chain helpers), their tests, + the 33 backfilled `docs/frds/*/work-orders/wo-*.md` frontmatters. ## 2026-06-24 â€” Observabilidad timeline: estimated `source: "git"` fallback (real order/dates/outcomes, estimated durations) for projects with no track
**What:** Added a fourth precedence step to the timeline reader, between `track` and `structural`: when a project has **no `track.jsonl`** but its **git history records the build** (WO-tagged commits), `readBuildTimeline` reconstructs an **estimated** timeline (`source: "git"`, `estimated: true`). New pure, tested `deriveGitTimeline(commits, orders)` (+ a fail-soft `git log` reader via `execSync`): it takes each WO id's **latest commit time** (real finish), orders the WOs by it (real build sequence), reads each WO's **final state from the orders** (real outcome) and counts the commits per WO as **attempts** (reopens); **durations are estimated** from the gap to the previous WO's commit, **clamped** to [1, 60] min and laid out **sequentially** so multi-day pauses don't blow up the axis. `TimelineView` renders it in the durations layout under an explicit **"â‰ˆ tiempos estimados (reconstruidos de git)"** banner (`data-mode="estimated"`), the legend switches to "duraciأ³n estimada", and the FRD-NN slug is derived from the WO id when the order is missing.
**Why:** Owner: MC was built before the track existed, so it only showed the honest *structural* view (states, no bars). He wanted it to "look like it happened" with calculated/estimated times â€” explicitly accepting approximate durations as long as they're clearly flagged. Git already holds the real provenance (117 WO-tagged commits for MC: order, dates, outcomes); only the per-WO *duration* is an estimate, and it's labeled as such. Honest, not fabricated.
**Verified:** biome/tsc clean; `deriveGitTimeline` unit-tested (null when no WO commit, FRDâ–¸WO order, 12-min gap â†’ 12 min, 24h gap â†’ clamped 60, attempts = commit count, frd-NN fallback, unsortedâ†’ordered); live (dev :3000) MC observabilidad renders `data-mode="estimated"` with the banner, 30 FRDs, 117 WO bars (8m/23m/60mâ€¦), states "Hecho آ· N intentos", zero console errors.
**Impact:** `src/lib/build-track/build-track.ts` (+ `BuildTimeline.estimated?`, `deriveGitTimeline` + git-log reader + helpers; tests), `_observability/TimelineView/TimelineView.tsx` (estimated banner + legend + `data-mode`). Canonical: **FRD-12 AC-12-003.1a** (precedence trackâ†’gitâ†’structuralâ†’empty; estimates always flagged). Manual: `concepts/estado-y-archivos` + `concepts/mission-control-por-dentro`. MC-only â€” no factory/plugin change.

## 2026-06-23 â€” DAG: zoom/pan (buttons + mouse wheel) + node text that fits the card
**What:** The Observabilidad â†’ DAG (`WoDag`) was legible only in theory: a wide graph (79 nodes) was auto-shrunk to **~0.45أ—** by `maxWidth:100% + height:auto`, so it rendered tiny, and the SVG `<text>` node titles (a hard `slice(0,18)`) spilled **3â€“8px past the card edge**. Two fixes: **(1) Zoom/pan** â€” the SVG now renders at natural size inside a bounded, scrollable viewport; a floating toolbar (zoom out آ· % readout that resets to 100% آ· zoom in آ· fit-to-view) AND the **mouse wheel** (zoom-to-cursor, `preventDefault` so the page doesn't scroll) drive a `scale` 0.3أ—â€“2.5أ—. The dataâ†’layout pipeline is memoized so zooming never recomputes the graph. **(2) Node legibility** â€” the title + `id آ· FRD` sub-line moved into a `<foreignObject>` HTML block that **wraps the title to â‰¤2 lines with ellipsis** (never overflowing) and **strips the redundant `WO-NN-MMM â€”` id prefix** from the title (the id shows once, in the mono sub-line); the node box grew 150أ—54â†’170أ—62 for the second line. Extracted `DagNodeGroup.tsx`, `ZoomControls.tsx`, `useDagZoom.ts` so `WoDag.tsx` stays under the 500-line cap.
**Follow-up â€” grab-to-pan (owner: "navegar estأ، difأ­cil, solo por el scroll â€¦ que pueda hacer clic y desplazarme mientras mantengo el clic"):** added press-and-drag panning over the canvas (`grab`/`grabbing` cursor, `userSelect:none`). Drag listeners live on `window` so a drag keeps tracking past the viewport edge; a press that travels past a 4px threshold marks `didPan` and a capture-phase click handler swallows the trailing click, so dragging never selects a node while a pure click still does. Scrollbar-gutter presses are ignored.
**Follow-up â€” fullscreen (owner: "una opciأ³n de full screen â€¦ ver todo en pantalla completa"):** added a toolbar toggle (`ti-maximize`/`ti-minimize`, after fit, with a divider) that fullscreens the whole DAG panel â€” legend + controls + canvas â€” via the browser Fullscreen API (new `useFullscreen` hook on a `panelRef`, guarded so it's a safe no-op where the API is absent). In fullscreen the panel becomes a flex column and the canvas flex-grows to fill the screen (`maxHeight` dropped); zoom/pan/fit keep working at the larger size; Escape or the toggle exits.
**Fix â€” fullscreen crashed on non-Chromium (owner hit it live):** `el.requestFullscreen()` returns a Promise per spec but some engines (WebKit/Safari, some WebViews) return `undefined`, so `.catch` on the raw return threw `Cannot read properties of undefined (reading 'catch')` and broke the render. Hardened `useFullscreen` to wrap the call in `Promise.resolve(...).catch()` (safe whether or not a Promise comes back), a `try/catch` for engines that throw synchronously when blocked, and `webkit*` fallbacks (element/exit + `webkitfullscreenchange`) so the state syncs on Safari too. Verified live by mocking `requestFullscreen` to return undefined / throw / reject â€” all three now "called, no throw".
**Layout bug this uncovered + fixed:** rendering the DAG at natural width exposed that the portfolio workspace **grid item** (`portfolio-page-workspace`) kept its default `min-width:auto` â€” which the track's `minmax(0,1fr)` floor does NOT override â€” so a wide child forced the pane past the page frame and the **whole page scrolled sideways**. Added `min-width:0` on the grid item (pairs with the track floor); now wide content (the DAG, a long timeline/table) scrolls inside its own container.
**Why:** Owner: "en â€¦ dag â€¦ todo estأ، muy chiquito â€¦ agregar una opciأ³n de Zoom â€¦ que funcione tambiأ©n con el scroll del mouse â€¦ los cards â€¦ mأ،s ancho o â€¦ los textos se hagan wrap hacia abajo, porque â€¦ se escapan del card."
**Verified:** Live (dev :3000, 1440أ—900): DAG at natural scale (was 0.448أ—); zoom 100%â†’fit 36% (fits the container), wheel 100%â†’115% with `preventDefault`; page never scrolls horizontally (grid `240px 946px`, container 856 with internal scroll); node text 20px inside the card edge, 2-line wrap. **Grab-to-pan:** a drag moves the scroll +120/+80 (`grab`â†’`grabbing`â†’`grab`), a drag over a node does NOT select it while a pure click does. **Fullscreen:** the toolbar toggle is present (`ti-maximize`, "Ver en pantalla completa"; `document.fullscreenEnabled` true), the click is crash-free, and the fullscreen layout fills the viewport (canvas 810/900px) â€” the Fullscreen API needs a genuine user gesture, so entering fullscreen is exercised in a real browser, not the automated preview. `tsc` + `biome` clean; **54 vitest green in WoDag** (incl. `useDagZoom`, `useFullscreen`, node-wrap/strip, pan/zoom toolbar) atop the portfolio+observability suites.
**Impact:** `WoDag/{WoDag.tsx, layout.ts, DagNodeGroup.tsx (new), ZoomControls.tsx (new), useDagZoom.ts (new), useFullscreen.ts (new)}` + tests; `portfolio/page.tsx` (`min-width:0` on the workspace grid item); FRD-12 **AC-12-004.5/.6** (new). Coordinated with the parallel responsive-grid pass (`.pc-portfolio-grid`, globals.css) â€” same root cause, complementary fix.

## 2026-06-23 â€” Pipeline redefinition: 5 phases, `release` = launched, new `deploy_target` (DR-085, factory-wide)
**What:** Reworked Mission Control to the new factory lifecycle (factory DR-085). The pipeline is now **5 project phases** â€” `product â†’ design â†’ architecture â†’ implementation â†’ release` â€” that map 1:1 to La Campaأ±a's 6 rooms (research is pre-project). **`operation` is removed**: a project at `phase: release` IS launched/live, and the old "operation" semantics (post-launch iteration, review-launch, "shipped" KPIs/achievements) now key off `release`. The audit/security/quality/metrics work conceptually moved into construction (it's the factory skills' concern; MC just reflects the phases). New status field **`deploy_target: internal | external`** (DR-085): a release is the same concept whether deployed to an external host (Vercel/AWS) or used as an internal tool (Mission Control on 127.0.0.1) â€” only the destination differs. Changes: `Phase` union drops `operation` + adds `DeployTarget`/`deployTarget` (parsed in `readStatus`); `deriveColumn` `release â†’ shipped` ("6 Release" column, was "building"/"5 Construcciأ³n"); `phaseFromProjectPhase` `release â†’ 5` (the Release room â€” **supersedes** the 2026-06-22 `releaseâ†’4` mapping below); the `operationâ†’release` semantics swept across ~15 app/lib files (board, campaign, portfolio, kpis, pulse, gamification, achievements, self-suggest, next-step, card, ProjectRail, PortfolioTable, CardDetail, workspace-header) + their tests. `deploy_target` is **surfaced**: a chip in the campaign's Release ficha (`CampaignPipeline` ficha header, threaded boardâ†’BoardShellâ†’CardDetail) and next to the stage chip in the project `WorkspaceHeader`. MC's own `status.yaml` gains `deploy_target: internal`.
**Why:** Owner: *"release y operaciأ³n son lo mismoâ€¦ el concepto es un release de un producto de software, interno o externo; la auditorأ­a/calidad/seguridad es el أ؛ltimo paso de la construcciأ³n."* Separating "release" (the act) from "operation" (live) was an artificial split; folding them removes the confusion that surfaced when MC (an internal release) showed inconsistent phases. Done directly (factory + MC together, owner-approved scope) with the two-layer discipline.
**Verified:** `verify.sh` GREEN â€” tsc, biome, knip, madge, **321 vitest files**, 14 smoke, 14 visual, 4 responsive, 28 shell. Live (dev :3000): board shows MC in **"6 Release"** (was "5 Construcciأ³n"); the card-detail campaign shows **"6 آ· Release â€” FASE ACTUAL آ· interno"** (deploy chip); no console errors. All visual baselines regenerated to the current render (the column rename + DR-085 were within the `maxDiffPixelRatio: 0.02` tolerance, so `--update-snapshots` had been silently skipping them â€” forced an exact regen at tolerance 0, then restored).
**Visual-test determinism (DR-085 follow-up):** the `inicio` baseline kept breaking on the env-dependent **plugin-drift banner** (FRD-15), which appears only mid-version-bump (installed < source, before `claude plugin update`). `e2e/visual.spec.ts` now collapses `[data-testid="dashboard-banners"]` before the screenshot, so health banners (drift + onboarding gate) never gate pixel diffs. Back-ported to the plugin stack template (DR-076) so `/pandacorp:upgrade` won't revert it.
**Impact:** `lib/status/status.ts` (Phase, DeployTarget, parsing), `lib/board/board.ts`, `lib/campaign/campaign.ts`, the ~15-file sweep + tests, `CampaignPipeline`/`CardDetail`/`BoardShell`/`board/page.tsx`/`IdeaBoardView` (deploy_target thread + chip), `workspace-header.tsx` + `ProjectWorkspace.tsx`, `e2e/visual.spec.ts` (+ template), all visual baselines, `.pandacorp/status.yaml`. Its transition is inline (the shared-Button pattern), since `globals.css` may only transition compositable props (AC-13-005.1).
- **A locked (not-yet-reached) phase's campaign ficha now shows its full info** â€” description, LEE/ESCRIBE, and the whole team â€” instead of a "ًں”’ esta fase no estأ، disponible" placeholder. The ficha is information *about* the phase; the header still marks a future phase "en espera". Only the build phase's **"Entrar a La Fragua" action** stays gated behind reaching build (info yes, action no).

**Why:** Owner: *"el botأ³n de descartar es un poco mأ،s grande que en el HTML y le falta un hover (distinto al del HTML, alineado con los otros como 'volver al tablero'). Y la info de abajo (la fase, los agentes) deberأ­a poder leerse siempre, aunque no hayas llegado a esa fase â€” es info de la fase, no veo sentido bloquearla."*

**Verified:** Live DOM â€” discard height 29px == back 29px, class `pc-discard` + transition present; a locked Release ficha shows header "6 آ· Release â€” en espera" + 2 team members, no locked marker, no forge action. `verify.sh` GREEN (incl. the `globals.css` non-compositable-transition adversarial gate, after moving the transition inline); no visual re-bless (both live only inside the open card detail).

**Impact:** `DiscardButton.tsx` (sm sizing + `.pc-discard` class + inline transition), `globals.css` (`.pc-discard:hover`), `CampaignPipeline.tsx` (dropped the locked-ficha early return + `FICHA_LOCKED_STYLE`; forge button gated on `phaseState !== "locked"`). Canonical: **AC-02-010.7** rewritten + [frd-02 amendment](frds/frd-02-ideas-board/frd.md). Tests updated to the new locked-ficha contract.

## 2026-06-22 â€” Inicio titleâ†’section gap actually fixed (the earlier `:empty` collapse never fired)
**What:** The gap between the Inicio `PageTitle` and "Desde tu أ؛ltima visita" was still **40px** (vs 16px on every other page) when no banner shows. The earlier fix added `[data-testid="dashboard-banners"]:empty { display:none }`, but the wrapper kept its `display:flex` from an **inline** `style={BANNERS_STYLE}` â€” and an inline declaration beats a CSS rule, so `:empty` never won; the empty (0-height) div stayed a flex item and the parent's `gap:24px` was applied (16 + 24 = 40). Moved the banner stack's layout into a **`.dashboard-banners` CSS class** (flex/gap there, not inline) so `.dashboard-banners:empty { display:none }` actually collapses it. Measured after: Inicio titleâ†’section gap = **16px**, identical to Portfolio (16px) and the other PageLayout pages.

**Why:** Owner re-flagged it: *"el espacio entre el tأ­tulo de Inicio y آ«Desde tu أ؛ltima visitaآ» es demasiado grande cuando no hay alerta â€” que sea exactamente igual a tablero/portafolio/propuestas."* Root cause was the inline-vs-CSS specificity trap; the honest correction also notes the prior pass **claimed** it fixed (eyeballed a screenshot) without measuring â€” it wasn't.

**Verified:** Live DOM measure â€” `dashboard-banners` computed `display:none` when empty; Inicio gap 16px == Portfolio gap 16px. `verify.sh` GREEN; `inicio` baseline re-blessed.

**Impact:** `globals.css` (`.dashboard-banners` + `:empty`), `page.tsx` (`style` â†’ `className`, removed the `BANNERS_STYLE` const). Lesson captured: inline `display` beats a CSS `:empty`/`:hover` rule â€” put the base layout in a class so the pseudo-class can win; and **measure** spacing, don't eyeball.

## 2026-06-22 â€” Plugin-sync banner: version-based, not SHA-based (kills the permanent false "behind")
**What:** The "El plugin instalado estأ، atrأ،s" banner (FRD-15) was **always on**, even right after a successful `claude plugin update`. Root cause: FRD-15 compared git **commit SHAs** â€” the installed `gitCommitSha` from `~/.claude/plugins/installed_plugins.json` vs `git log -1 -- plugin/`. But `installed_plugins.json.gitCommitSha` is **frozen at install time** and does NOT advance when `claude plugin update` runs (it updates `version` + `lastUpdated`, not the SHA), while the compared HEAD advanced on **every** `plugin/` commit. So in the factory â€” where `plugin/` is committed constantly â€” installed (`a95037f`, June-15) was permanently "behind" HEAD (`6f54a30`) even though the installed plugin was version 8.42.0 == source 8.42.0. Diagnosed live: `/api/plugin-sync` returned `reason:"behind"` while `claude plugin update` reported up-to-date.

Reworked FRD-15 to be **semver-version-based** â€” the SAME signal `claude plugin update` uses:
- `lib/plugin-sync.ts` rewritten: `readInstalledVersion` (installed_plugins.json `version`) + `readPluginSourceVersion` (`plugin/.claude-plugin/plugin.json` `version`) + a semver comparator. Removed the git/SHA/dirty readers (`readInstalledSha`/`readPluginHeadSha`/`readPluginDirty`/`shaEqual`) and the `execFileSync`/git dependency entirely. New `PluginSyncState`: `{ installedVersion, sourceVersion, drift, reason: "behind"|"in-sync"|"unknown", detail }`.
- Banner fires **only** on `reason:"behind"` (installed strictly older than source). Equal/newer â†’ `in-sync` â†’ nothing. Unreadable/unparseable â†’ `unknown` â†’ nothing (no false alarm). The component (`plugin-sync-banner.tsx`) simplified to one constant heading + recall (the 3 reason-variants â€” uncommitted/both â€” are gone).

**Why (owner decision):** *"tengo la أ؛ltima versiأ³nâ€¦ corrأ­ `claude plugin update` y dice que estoy actualizado, آ؟por quأ© me sigue lanzando ese mensaje? que solo se muestre cuando realmente falta actualizar."* The owner chose **version-behind only** as the trigger (asked explicitly): uncommitted-`plugin/`-edits is NOT a trigger, because in the factory `plugin/` is edited constantly and that would be permanently noisy. Version-behind is exactly "needs `claude plugin update`". This reverses FRD-15's old "never use the semver version" invariant â€” that invariant was the bug, given `gitCommitSha` is unmaintained.

**Verified (browser + gate):** `/api/plugin-sync` now returns `{installedVersion:"8.42.0", sourceVersion:"8.42.0", drift:false, reason:"in-sync", detail:"instalado v8.42.0 آ· plugin al dأ­a"}`; browser-confirmed the banner is **gone** on `/` (dashboard-banners has 0 children). Drift path covered by tests (installed < source â†’ behind). `verify.sh` GREEN (plugin-sync suites rewritten version-based: lib 30 + route 19 + banner 33; the 3 obsolete SHA/dirty/git adversarial suites deleted). `inicio` visual baseline re-blessed (banner removed).

**Impact:** `lib/plugin-sync/plugin-sync.ts` (full rewrite), `plugin-sync-banner.tsx` (simplified), `api/plugin-sync/route.ts` (unchanged â€” returns the new state). Tests: `plugin-sync.test.ts` rewritten; `route.test.ts`/`route.integration.adversarial.test.ts` + the 2 banner suites adapted; 3 SHA/dirty/git adversarial suites deleted. Canonical: **FRD-15** (amended â€” version-based EARS), `architecture.md`, `api.md` (WO-15-001 superseded note). Generator â‰  verifier preserved (tests adapted by separate agents, re-run independently).

## 2026-06-22 â€” "Tu progreso" XP bar: full-width track (was the tiny 90px topbar bar)
**What:** The level/XP bar in the dashboard "Tu progreso" foot rendered as a tiny 90أ—9px stub. It was using `XpBar size="compact"` â€” the inline variant meant for the GuildBar topbar â€” instead of the prototype's full `.xpbar` (index.html ~L741: 18px tall, **full width**). Added a third `XpBar` size, **`size="track"`** (full-width 18px bar, no label rows), and pointed `Progreso` at it. `Progreso` already renders its own NVآ·title + XP/next label row above the bar (faithful to the prototype foot), so the bar variant must be label-less. Extracted the shared `FullTrack` so `full` and `track` use one track definition (DR-057 / rule-of-three).

**Why:** *"esa barrita estأ، superchiquitaâ€¦ en el HTML es grande, gruesoâ€¦ estando vacأ­o deberأ­a ocupar todo el ancho"* â€” even at 0 XP the track must occupy its full width at the prototype thickness. The fill is honestly 0% (no fake fill, FRD-09), but the track is now full-width 18px.

**Verified:** DOM measure of the bar in `progreso-strip` = 18px tall أ— full-width (was 9أ—90); browser-confirmed on `/`. `verify.sh` GREEN (325 test files incl. a new `size="track"` XpBar suite; smoke/visual/responsive/shell). `inicio` visual baseline re-blessed; `logros` (GuildHero `full` XpBar) unchanged by the `FullTrack` extraction.

**Impact:** `XpBar.tsx` (+`track` variant, `FullTrack` extraction), `Progreso.tsx` (`compact`â†’`track`), `XpBar.test.tsx` (+track suite). Canonical: `docs/design/components.md` (XpBar row).

**What:** Owner QA on `/` found the health alerts (PluginSyncBanner FRD-15 + OrphansBanner FRD-16) diverged from the approved prototype (`docs/design/prototype/index.html` `bBanner`/`.cmd`). Brought the **shared primitives** back in line (one fix, all banners):

## 2026-06-22 â€” Documentation upgrade: the Manual is now a navigable, "for-dummies" interactive graph (FRD-08)
**What:** Reworked the Documentation surface from a file-reference (raw English frontmatter + a `<pre>` dump of the `SKILL.md`) into the **navigable, visual, plain-language graph** the owner asked for. Three parts:

- **Curated, for-dummies layer.** New hand-authored **`skill-flows`** (`src/lib/manual/skill-flows.ts`): a Spanish, plain-language **explainer** + the typed flow for **all 23 skills**, authored from the real `plugin/skills/<slug>/SKILL.md` bodies + the decision rules (accuracy contract, DR-046). `SkillDetail` now shows the explainer (wins over the English frontmatter description) + the `FlowGraph` + the full `SKILL.md` rendered as **markdown** in a collapsible â€” never again a raw `<pre>` dump.

Mobile `/manual` reflows with no horizontal overflow (`target_platforms` stays `desktop`; mobile polish is Phase B). ## 2026-06-22 â€” Whole-app fidelity pass: make MC identical to the prototype, working & coherent
**What:** A full sweep to make every surface (a) pixel-faithful to the approved prototype (`docs/design/prototype/index.html`), (b) actually functional, and (c) coherent. Audited the whole prototype + FRDs, inventoried visual **and** functional defects (`.pandacorp/run/fidelity-plan.md`), then fixed foundation-first and repainted per surface (parallel Opus agents per surface; an independent reviewer â‰  the generators), verifying each route in the browser against the prototype, in dark + light, interacting (search/tabs/filters/copy/navigation), with a clean console.

Decisions (the why):
- **DEC-1 آ· single 1240px container.** The prototype wraps topbar **and** content in one `#pcapp{max-width:1240px;margin:0 auto;padding:24px 20px 60px}`; MC had the topbar in a 72rem wrapper and each page at a different width (content escaped the header). `AppShell` now wraps the header **and** `#main-content` in one 1240px column (both the normal and shell-exempt branches); per-page `maxWidth`/`margin`/outer-padding removed (Inicio, Propuestas, Logros, Portfolio). Canonical: FRD-19/`AppShell`.
- **DEC-2 آ· tokens = the prototype.** Light theme diverged in 5 values (`--color-text3/warn/cat-1/cat-6/cat-8`) and the `@media (prefers light)` block was missing `--color-cat-*`/shadows/backdrop; `globals.css` reconciled to the prototype hex (dark already matched). Four never-declared tokens consumers referenced (`--color-text-muted/canvas/border2/surface-panel`) are now compatibility aliases in `:root` â†’ resolve to the real prototype tokens, cascading across light/dark.
- **DEC-3 آ· Configuration IA.** The prototype has **no** Config tab â€” config lives inside Manualâ†’Referencia. The 6-tab nav is already correct; `/configuration` is kept as a deep-link / cross-nav target, and Manualâ†’Referencia is the canonical in-nav surface (both reuse the same DR-046-derived components â€” no duplicated logic).
- **DEC-4 آ· workspace embedded in Portfolio.** The prototype's Portfolio = rail + `projectPane` (the whole project workspace) on the right; MC had a stub placeholder + a separate full-screen `/projects/[slug]`. Factored a shared **`ProjectWorkspace`** (normal flow) rendered by BOTH the Portfolio right pane (`WorkspaceSlot`) and `/projects/[slug]`. `TabBar` merges into the current query (so `?project=` survives tab switches inside Portfolio); the snapshot panel moved INTO the Summary tab (WS-2); the running pip is wired (WS-3); the workspace title is `<h1>` standalone / `<h2>` embedded (one `<h1>` per page). Canonical: FRD-03/FRD-04.
- **DEC-5 آ· Party honest.** Party + Campaign render the live RPG map from real events; no active build â†’ a guided empty state, never broken.

Data-layer root-cause fixes (FRD-01) â€” the dominant one reopened half the app:
- **`portfolio.ts`** parsed only EN headers but the real `factory/portfolio.md` is gitignored â†’ Spanish, so `readPortfolio()` returned `[]` â†’ Portfolio + Workspace + Party + home cartera + Logros/XP all dark. Now maps ES **and** EN headers, cleans the backtick/prose path cell, and maps Spanish advisory phases; regression-locked with a Spanish-shape test. `resolveProjectPath` moved to `config.ts` (so consumers resolve paths without importing â€” and being mocked out by â€” the portfolio module; the workspace had been reading status from the raw relative cell against cwd â†’ empty status). Also: `ideas.ts` `project:""`â†’undefined; `standards.ts` adds `design.md`; `reference.ts` adds `librarian` + a `sync-portfolio` runsIn pattern.
- **Digest coherence (FRD-18):** the "Desde tu أ؛ltima visita" digest flooded with thousands of raw `SubagentStop` infra events. Added `filterDigestEvents` (drops SubagentStop/SupervisorTick/AgentWorking noise) + Spanish milestone labels â†’ real change events.
- **Manual (FRD-08):** was plain `react-markdown` with no prose styling and **zero** of the 10 inline diagrams. Now renders each Concept/Guide/Landing/Quickstart as React (DocH accent-bar headings + `.panel` cards + `CmdRow`) with all 10 diagram components (in `src/components/modules/manual-diagrams/`) + the 7 prototype guides. Reference still derives from canonical source (DR-046). *Known P2:* derived skill/agent descriptions show the canonical English frontmatter (vs the prototype's Spanish) â€” a consequence of derive-don't-copy.

**Why:** Repeated "it's done" turned out false because nothing was browser-verified against the prototype, and the visual gate proves *consistency* with its own (broken-layout-era) baseline, not *fidelity*. This pass verifies every route in the browser against the prototype itself, interacting, and only re-blesses baselines after that confirmation. The per-FRD mock specs + an independent reviewer (generator â‰  verifier) are the durable process improvement.

## 2026-06-22 â€” Re-anchor Phase A: built the missing global app shell (FRD-19) + Shell-Presence Gate is real & GREEN
**What:** Built the persistent top-navigation shell the per-FRD sharding (DR-056) had left orphaned â€” `layout.tsx` previously mounted only `GuildBar` + a loose `ProposalsBadge`, with **no menu at all** ("the menu doesn't even appear").
